						}

					set_technology = {

						sup_delay = 0
						pocket_defence = 0
						grand_battle_plan = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

							has_tech = mass_assault

					}

					}
				}
			}

	icon = GFX_goal_HIP_SIR_SNA_musical_research
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = HIP_SIR_the_child_king
	cost = 3
	prerequisite = {
		focus = HIP_SIR_the_child_king
	}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				character = HIP_SIR_sonata
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_has_deficit
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 150
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus HIP_SIR_the_musical_rnd_department"
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = magical_facility_construction_tt
			temp_facility_state_loc = "[1165.GetName]"
			temp_facility_province_loc = "[1165.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					1165 = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						can_construct_building = magical_facility
					}
				}
				1165 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = magical_facility
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
						province = 19886
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_research_unlocked
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_siren_research_tt
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = HIP_SIR_expand_the_systems
	icon = GFX_goal_HIP_SIR_SNA_expand_systems
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = HIP_SIR_dunes_of_zarantia
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = HIP_SIR_dunes_of_zarantia
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = HIP_SIR_a_mistake_rectified
	}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				character = HIP_SIR_sonata
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_has_deficit
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 150
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus HIP_SIR_expand_the_systems"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_SIR_musical_patronage
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_SIR_musical_patronage
				add_idea = HIP_SIR_musical_patronage_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_low
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_low
				add_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_low_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_high
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_high
				add_idea = HIP_SIR_siren_healthcare_high_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = { pre_HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_factory = -0.05 } # this is times 10 the final value for calcualtions
				add_to_variable = { pre_HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_dockyard = -0.05 } # this is times 10 the final value for calcualtions
				add_to_variable = { pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_morale_factor = -0.05 } # this is times 10 the final value for calcualtions
				add_to_variable = { pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_attack_factor = -0.05 } # this is times 10 the final value for calcualtions
				add_to_variable = { pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_defence_factor = -0.05 } # this is times 10 the final value for calcualtions
				set_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_factory = pre_HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_factory }
				set_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_dockyard = pre_HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_dockyard }
				set_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_morale_factor = pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_morale_factor }
				set_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_attack_factor = pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_attack_factor }
				set_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_defence_factor = pre_HIP_MAGIC_army_defence_factor }

				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_consumer_goods_factor = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_conscription = -0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_recruitable_seapony_pop = -0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = -0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = -0.01 }
				divide_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_factory = 10 }
				divide_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_industrial_capacity_dockyard = -0.005 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_org_factor = -0.01 }
				divide_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_morale_factor = 10 }
				divide_variable= { HIP_MAGIC_army_attack_factor = 10 }
				divide_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_army_defence_factor = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { HIP_MAGIC_magic_drift = 2 }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { HIP_SIR_sonata_power = 1 }
	}
}
